Section 1:
SB146 ENROLLED

First Read: 14-Jan-26
SB146 Enrolled
2 To make appropriations for the ordinary expenses of the
3 executive, legislative, and judicial agencies of the State,
4 for other functions of government, for debt service, and for
5 capital outlay for the fiscal year ending September 30, 2027.
6 BE IT ENACTED BY THE LEGISLATURE OF ALABAMA:
7 Section 1. The monies in Section 3 are appropriated
8 from the named funds for the 2027 fiscal year to the state
9 agencies indicated, as the amounts to be used to pay the
10 expenditures of the named agencies, and are in lieu of all
11 monies appropriated for these purposes in other sections of
12 the Alabama Statutes.
13 For the purpose of this act, the amounts herein for
14 expenditures are listed by programmatic area and the totals
15 for all programs are shown by the source of funds. It is
16 intended that only the herein named funds be appropriated in
17 the amounts specified to the named agencies and that the
18 following definitions shall be applicable.
19 "Total" shall mean the aggregate total appropriation of
20 all funding sources.
21 "Program" shall mean specific governmental services
22 required to achieve a specific objective. A program shall be
23 directed to meeting the need of an identified clientele, or
24 group of recipients or beneficiaries, and shall be expended
25 only for such purposes.
26 "Capital Outlay" shall mean expenditures which result
27 in the acquisition and/or addition to items, such as land or
Page 1
in the acquisition and/or addition to items, such as land or
SB146 Enrolled
28 buildings, which have an appreciable and calculable period of
29 usefulness in excess of one year, and shall be expended only
30 for such purposes.
31 "Debt Service" shall mean an expenditure for the
32 payment of interest and principal on bonded debt obligations
33 of the State, and shall be expended only for such purposes.
34 "Federal and Local Funds" shall mean all gifts, grants,
35 contributions, or entitlements, including grants by the
36 Congress of the United States, municipalities or counties.
37 Section 2. (a) There is hereby appropriated the amounts
38 set forth herein for the ordinary expenses of the executive,
39 legislative, and judicial agencies of the State, for other
40 functions of government, for debt service, and for capital
41 outlay for the fiscal year ending September 30, 2027, to be
42 paid out of any monies hereinafter specified, from such other
43 funds and accounts as may be designated, or so much thereof as
44 may be necessary, and the total amount to be expended for the
45 items for which the appropriation is herein made shall not
46 exceed the amount provided therefor, except as provided in the
47 Budget Management Act of 1976, Sections 41-19-1 through
48 41-19-12, Code of Alabama 1975. Provided, however, that
49 regardless of the ending date of any pay period which has been
50 or may be established by the Legislature for the payment of
51 salaries of state employees, the entire payment due shall be
52 made from the fiscal year's appropriation in which the pay
53 date falls.
54 (b) All appropriations made in Section 3 shall be at
Page 2
(b) All appropriations made in Section 3 shall be at
SB146 Enrolled
55 the program level. Any directed expenditure of funds below a
56 program shall be from funds appropriated for the program.
Page 3
program shall be from funds appropriated for the program.

193 In accordance with Sections 12-19-310 through 12-19-315, Code of Alabama 1975.
194 During fiscal year 2027, and notwithstanding any provision of law to the
195 contrary, the Chief Justice of the Supreme Court of Alabama may transfer up to
196 $12,000,000 from local discretionary funds managed by circuit clerks and
197 circuit and district judges, including Circuit Clerk’s Funds, Circuit Clerk’s
198 Judicial Administration Funds, and Presiding Judge Judicial Administration
199 Funds. The Chief Justice may require each circuit clerk or judge responsible
200 for the administration of such funds to remit to the Administrative Office of
201 Courts a graduated proportional share of the available balances of such funds.
202 The Chief Justice may establish the schedule, methodology, and date used to
203 determine the balances subject to transfer, and any amounts expended after
204 that date that would otherwise reduce the balances subject to transfer may be
205 included in calculating the required remittance. Any funds transferred
206 pursuant to this section shall be remitted to the Administrative Director of
207 Courts for deposit into the State Judicial Administration Fund and used for
208 the operational expenses of the Unified Judicial System in fiscal year 2027.
209 Total Unified Judicial System 189,807,354 56,033,204 245,840,558

314 Enforcement Fund
315 Total Alcoholic Beverage Control 168,991,169 168,991,169
316 Board, Alabama
317 In addition to the above appropriation herein made, there is hereby appropriated for
318 each additional retail and wholesale store that is relocated or put into operation
319 during the fiscal year, an amount equal to the sum required to install and operate a
320 comparable store in operation by said Board. There is further appropriated to the
321 Alabama Alcoholic Beverage Control Board, after provision has been made for the
322 other expenditures herein authorized, such sums as are or may be necessary to
323 purchase the alcoholic beverages which are essential to maintain adequate stocks and
324 inventory for an economic and successful sales operation. In addition to the above
325 appropriation, it is further provided that, in the event any county or municipality
326 of the state shall, during the fiscal period covered by this appropriation by proper
327 referendum, authorize the legal sale of malt and brewed beverages within such county
328 or municipality, there is further appropriated, in addition to the amount herein set
329 out, an amount comparable to that expended during the prior fiscal year for beer and
330 license tax supervision within counties or municipalities of similar size and
331 population. Provided further, that the amount appropriated herein shall be reduced
332 in like manner in the event any county or municipality wherein malt and brewed
333 beverages are now authorized by law to be sold shall, during the fiscal period
334 covered by this appropriation by proper referendum, declare unlawful the sale in
335 such county or municipality of such malt or brewed beverages. Notwithstanding any
336 other laws to the contrary, all revenue generated from bailment fees shall remain
337 with the Board to be used for its operations.

1399 For award payments to licensed physicians or nurse practitioners who agree
1400 to practice full-time in primary care in a medically underserved rural area
1401 for an agreed upon number of years. No payment shall be allowed for a
1402 physician or nurse practitioner who has practiced within three years of
1403 October 1, 2026, in a primary care service area with a deficit, or surplus
1404 of less than 2.0 primary-care physicians, as shown by the most-recent Status
1405 Report of the Alabama Primary Care Physician Workforce from the Office for
1406 Family Health Education & Research at the UAB Huntsville Regional Medical
1407 Campus. The Office of Primary Care and Rural Health may pay an eligible
1408 physician or nurse practitioner as much as $50,000 a year for each year of
1409 service, in a medically underserved rural area, agreed to by contract by the
1410 physician or nurse practitioner, but any payment shall be for no more than
1411 three years. Contracts shall set out refund and penalty requirements for
1412 failure by a physician or nurse practitioner to meet the contract terms. A
1413 medically underserved rural area as determined by the Office shall be: (1)
1414 in a rural primary care service area with a deficit of primary-care
1415 physicians as shown by the most recent Status Report of the Alabama Primary
1416 Care Physician Workforce, and (2) in a county in which no more than two
1417 physicians have worked or are scheduled to be working within 12 months to
1418 repay a loan awarded by the Alabama Board of Medical Scholarship Awards. The
1419 Office shall file a report with the Chairs of the Senate Committee on
1420 Finance and Taxation-General Fund and the House Ways and Means-General Fund
1421 Committee, the Legislative Fiscal Officer and the Finance Director by
1422 October 15, 2027, on how the money was spent in fiscal year 2027 and the
1423 names of participants and where they agreed to practice or were practicing
1424 in return for payments from the Office.

1481 To award matching grants for ambulances for emergency medical services
1482 operating in rural counties. The Office may consider requests for matching
1483 grants to buy an ambulance, rapid-response vehicle, or cardiac monitor or
1484 other durable medical equipment to be placed in an ambulance or

1486 The Office may award a grant equal to no more than 75 percent of the cost of

1978 The Medicaid Agency will reimburse the Department of Public Health for
1979 actual costs (in compliance with OMB Circular A-87 and Centers for Medicare
1980 and Medicaid Services guidelines) for services provided. The Department of
1981 Public Health shall transfer to the Medicaid Agency the state funds
1982 attributable to the difference between their costs and Medicaid's routine
1983 reimbursement fee. The Medicaid Agency shall make every effort to maintain
1984 level funding for the adult prosthetic and orthotic program in fiscal year
1985 2027. Any requirements for prior authorization of antipsychotic drugs will be
1986 for the limited purpose of managing off-label utilization. The Medicaid Agency
1987 shall make every effort to provide access for medications prescribed in
1988 accordance with FDA approved indications for mental illness and HIV/AIDS. The
1989 Alabama Medicaid Agency shall not pay for a generic drug that is more
1990 expensive than its brand name drug, net of rebates. The Alabama Medicaid
1991 Agency shall continue to fund and support the PACE program in accordance with
1992 written agreements.

2751 Total Revenue, Department of 463,000 229,166,353 229,629,353
2752 The amounts hereinabove appropriated for the cost of maintenance and operations of
2753 the Department of Revenue are in lieu of any other statutory provisions for the
2754 payment of the cost of operating said Department for collections of the taxes as
2755 authorized by law. Provided, however, in addition to the amount hereinabove
2756 appropriated, there is hereby appropriated to the Department of Revenue all sums
2757 allowed the Department of Revenue by acts of the Legislature as a charge for the
2758 collection of taxes or licenses. The Revenue Department shall not be limited in any
2759 way whatsoever in its ability to utilize or spend its full appropriation and all
2760 sums allowed to the Department of Revenue by acts of the Legislature as a charge for
2761 the collection of taxes or licenses. It is the intent of the Legislature that the
2762 Department of Revenue utilize the appropriations made to it in this act to: (1)
2763 significantly reduce the amount of delinquent taxes owed to the state; (2) employ
2764 sufficient examiners and audit personnel to ensure that taxes owed to the state are
2765 collected accurately and timely; and (3) update its personal computers and related
2766 equipment to become more efficient in the collection of taxes owed to the state.
2767 During Fiscal Year 2027, the Department shall report semi-annually to the Chairs of
2768 the House Ways and Means-General Fund Committee and Senate Finance and
2769 Taxation-General Fund Committee, and the Legislative Fiscal Officer on all actions
2770 taken by the Department in furtherance of these goals. The reports shall include,
2771 but not be limited to: (1) the number and amount of delinquent taxes collected
2772 during the quarter and the number and amounts of delinquent taxes outstanding as of
2773 the end of the quarter; (2) the number of additional examiners and audit personnel
2774 employed during the quarter (not including examiners and audit personnel employed to
2775 replace personnel that retire or otherwise leave state service); and (3) the number
2776 of new personal computers and related equipment put into use during the quarter.

2826 (c) Elderly Medication Program 1,758,636 1,758,636
2827 The Alabama SenioRx program shall provide assistance obtaining prescription
2828 medications and shall be expanded to allow comprehensive benefits screening
2829 and application assistance through an Area Agency on Aging designated by the
2830 Department as an Aging and Disability Resource Center (ADRC). It is the intent
2831 of the Legislature that applicants apply through local Area Agencies on Aging
2832 and their provider networks to ensure services are maximized and that
2833 paperwork and inconvenience to the clients are minimized to receive access to
2834 local and public benefits and prescription assistance. The Department of
2835 Senior Services shall report semi-annually to the Chairs of the House Ways and
2836 Means-General Fund Committee and the Senate Finance and Taxation-General Fund
2837 Committee, the Governor, the Director of Finance, and the Legislative Fiscal
2838 Officer. The reports shall include the number of clients served by an ADRC,
2839 the number of unduplicated SenioRx participants, the number of prescriptions
2840 filled, and the estimated value of the drugs provided.

3020 for such payment. There is also hereby appropriated an amount not to exceed
3021 $25,000,000 as an annual contribution to the Alabama Transportation
3022 Infrastructure Bank, if needed, for payment of debt service. The Director of
3023 Transportation, with the consent of the Governor and the Director of Finance,
3024 shall have the authority to transfer any appropriation or any portion thereof
3025 between and among subdivisions (a), (b) and (c) of this section whenever such
3026 transfer shall be necessary to assure maximum utilization of federal matching
3027 funds which shall become available. In the event that there shall not be
3028 sufficient funds available for payment of all appropriations hereinabove made,
3029 the following provisions shall be applicable. In the event of such
3030 insufficiency in respect of said revenues accruing to the Department of
3031 Transportation: (1) the appropriation made for Debt Service in subdivisions
3032 (a) and (b) hereof shall be paid in full, and (2) the appropriations from the
3033 revenues accruing to the Department of Transportation that are herein made for
3034 the purposes referred to in subdivisions (a), (b) and (c) except for Debt
3035 Service, hereof shall be allocated among the purposes referred to in said
3036 subdivisions in such order and with such priorities as the Director of the
3037 Department of Transportation shall from time to time direct. The funds
3038 appropriated in subdivisions (a) and (c) hereof, for the matching federal
3039 funds, shall not revert at the end of the fiscal year for which such
3040 appropriations are made but shall remain available for the purposes for which
3041 such appropriations were made. In addition to all appropriations hereinabove
3042 made, there is hereby appropriated to the Department of Transportation all
3043 federal funds accruing thereto to be expended only for the purpose for which
3044 such funds are made available.

3544 Section 4. In addition to the amounts otherwise
3545 appropriated in this act, there is hereby appropriated from
3546 the several funds in the State Treasury, except the Education
3547 Trust Fund, and in the same proportion as the salaries of the
3548 several State officials and employees are paid, such
3549 additional amounts as may be necessary to pay for a two
3550 percent (2%) salary increase enacted in the 2026 Regular
3551 Session. The additional amounts appropriated in this section
3552 from the State General Fund shall not exceed $16,000,000 for
3553 the fiscal year ending September 30, 2027. The Director of
3554 Finance shall ensure that first priority shall be given to all
3555 State General Fund payrolls, including the payroll of the
3556 Legislature. State agencies shall receive additional
3557 allocations from the appropriation made in this section from
3558 the State General Fund in amounts necessary to increase total
3559 salaries paid from the State General Fund by two percent. The
3560 remainder of this appropriation from the State General Fund
3561 may be allotted by the Director of Finance to those agencies
3562 which receive transfers from the State General Fund.

SB146 Enrolled
1 Enrolled, An Act,
2 To make appropriations for the ordinary expenses of the
3 executive, legislative, and judicial agencies of the State,
4 for other functions of government, for debt service, and for
5 capital outlay for the fiscal year ending September 30, 2027.
6 BE IT ENACTED BY THE LEGISLATURE OF ALABAMA:
7 Section 1. The monies in Section 3 are appropriated
8 from the named funds for the 2027 fiscal year to the state
9 agencies indicated, as the amounts to be used to pay the
10 expenditures of the named agencies, and are in lieu of all
11 monies appropriated for these purposes in other sections of
12 the Alabama Statutes.
13 For the purpose of this act, the amounts herein for
14 expenditures are listed by programmatic area and the totals
15 for all programs are shown by the source of funds. It is
16 intended that only the herein named funds be appropriated in
17 the amounts specified to the named agencies and that the
18 following definitions shall be applicable.
19 "Total" shall mean the aggregate total appropriation of
20 all funding sources.
21 "Program" shall mean specific governmental services
22 required to achieve a specific objective. A program shall be
23 directed to meeting the need of an identified clientele, or
24 group of recipients or beneficiaries, and shall be expended
25 only for such purposes.
26 "Capital Outlay" shall mean expenditures which result
27 in the acquisition and/or addition to items, such as land or
Page 1

in the acquisition and/or addition to items, such as land or
SB146 Enrolled
28 buildings, which have an appreciable and calculable period of
29 usefulness in excess of one year, and shall be expended only
30 for such purposes.
31 "Debt Service" shall mean an expenditure for the
32 payment of interest and principal on bonded debt obligations
33 of the State, and shall be expended only for such purposes.
34 "Federal and Local Funds" shall mean all gifts, grants,
35 contributions, or entitlements, including grants by the
36 Congress of the United States, municipalities or counties.
37 Section 2. (a) There is hereby appropriated the amounts
38 set forth herein for the ordinary expenses of the executive,
39 legislative, and judicial agencies of the State, for other
40 functions of government, for debt service, and for capital
41 outlay for the fiscal year ending September 30, 2027, to be
42 paid out of any monies hereinafter specified, from such other
43 funds and accounts as may be designated, or so much thereof as
44 may be necessary, and the total amount to be expended for the
45 items for which the appropriation is herein made shall not
46 exceed the amount provided therefor, except as provided in the
47 Budget Management Act of 1976, Sections 41-19-1 through
48 41-19-12, Code of Alabama 1975. Provided, however, that
49 regardless of the ending date of any pay period which has been
50 or may be established by the Legislature for the payment of
51 salaries of state employees, the entire payment due shall be
52 made from the fiscal year's appropriation in which the pay
53 date falls.
54 (b) All appropriations made in Section 3 shall be at

56 program shall be from funds appropriated for the program.

194 During fiscal year 2027, and notwithstanding any provision of law to the
195 contrary, the Chief Justice of the Supreme Court of Alabama may transfer up to
196 $12,000,000 from local discretionary funds managed by circuit clerks and
197 circuit and district judges, including Circuit Clerk’s Funds, Circuit Clerk’s
198 Judicial Administration Funds, and Presiding Judge Judicial Administration
199 Funds. The Chief Justice may require each circuit clerk or judge responsible
200 for the administration of such funds to remit to the Administrative Office of
201 Courts a graduated proportional share of the available balances of such funds.
202 The Chief Justice may establish the schedule, methodology, and date used to
203 determine the balances subject to transfer, and any amounts expended after
204 that date that would otherwise reduce the balances subject to transfer may be
205 included in calculating the required remittance. Any funds transferred
206 pursuant to this section shall be remitted to the Administrative Director of
207 Courts for deposit into the State Judicial Administration Fund and used for
208 the operational expenses of the Unified Judicial System in fiscal year 2027.

1016 It is the intent of the Legislature that all grants shall follow the standard and
1017 proper grant process and shall meet all departmental guidelines. The Director of the
1018 Alabama Department of Economic and Community Affairs shall report to the Chairs of
1019 the House Ways and Means-General Fund Committee and the Senate Finance and
1020 Taxation-General Fund Committee and the Legislative Fiscal Officer all funds and
1021 grants expended specifically in areas with high unemployment and low personal income
1022 levels. The report shall detail the amount of funds available in each program and
1023 the amount of funds expended in these targeted areas. The Director of the Alabama
1024 Department of Economic and Community Affairs shall report within thirty days after
1025 the end of each quarter all grants made by the Department in the previous quarter to
1026 the Chairs of the House Ways and Means-General Fund Committee and the Senate Finance
1027 and Taxation-General Fund Committee, and the Legislative Fiscal Officer. The report
1028 shall include the recipient of the grant, the source of funds for each grant, and
1029 the purpose of each grant. The Director of the Alabama Department of Economic and
1030 Community Affairs shall notify all members of the local legislative delegation five
1031 days prior to the announcement of any grant made to any entity located in the
1032 legislative jurisdiction. The five days prior notice requirement shall be waived in
1033 the event of a declared emergency. The Governor shall encourage the Department to
1034 disburse the funds provided herein on a nondiscriminatory basis.

1399 For award payments to licensed physicians or nurse practitioners who agree
1400 to practice full-time in primary care in a medically underserved rural area
1401 for an agreed upon number of years. No payment shall be allowed for a
1402 physician or nurse practitioner who has practiced within three years of
1403 October 1, 2026, in a primary care service area with a deficit, or surplus
1404 of less than 2.0 primary-care physicians, as shown by the most-recent Status
1405 Report of the Alabama Primary Care Physician Workforce from the Office for
1406 Family Health Education & Research at the UAB Huntsville Regional Medical
1407 Campus. The Office of Primary Care and Rural Health may pay an eligible
1408 physician or nurse practitioner as much as $50,000 a year for each year of
1409 service, in a medically underserved rural area, agreed to by contract by the
1410 physician or nurse practitioner, but any payment shall be for no more than
1411 three years. Contracts shall set out refund and penalty requirements for
1412 failure by a physician or nurse practitioner to meet the contract terms. A
1413 medically underserved rural area as determined by the Office shall be: (1)
1414 in a rural primary care service area with a deficit of primary-care
1415 physicians as shown by the most recent Status Report of the Alabama Primary
1416 Care Physician Workforce, and (2) in a county in which no more than two
1417 physicians have worked or are scheduled to be working within 12 months to
1418 repay a loan awarded by the Alabama Board of Medical Scholarship Awards. The
1419 Office shall file a report with the Chairs of the Senate Committee on
1420 Finance and Taxation-General Fund and the House Ways and Means-General Fund
1421 Committee, the Legislative Fiscal Officer and the Finance Director by
1422 October 15, 2027, on how the money was spent in fiscal year 2027 and the
1423 names of participants and where they agreed to practice or were practicing
1424 in return for payments from the Office.

1481 To award matching grants for ambulances for emergency medical services
1482 operating in rural counties. The Office may consider requests for matching
1483 grants to buy an ambulance, rapid-response vehicle, or cardiac monitor or
1484 other durable medical equipment to be placed in an ambulance or
1485 rapid-response vehicle, from a county, city, hospital, or ambulance service.
1486 The Office may award a grant equal to no more than 75 percent of the cost of
1487 the ambulance, rapid-response vehicle, or equipment, the percentage
1488 depending on the financial resources of the applicant and the need for the
1489 vehicle or equipment as judged by officials with the state’s regional
1490 emergency medical services offices. Preference shall be given to grants for
1491 an ambulance or rapid-response vehicle that would be based in a county with
1492 two or fewer ambulances. The Office shall file a report with the Chairs of
1493 the Senate Committee on Finance and Taxation-General Fund and the House Ways
1494 and Means-General Fund, the Legislative Fiscal Officer and the Finance

1978 The Medicaid Agency will reimburse the Department of Public Health for
1979 actual costs (in compliance with OMB Circular A-87 and Centers for Medicare
1980 and Medicaid Services guidelines) for services provided. The Department of
1981 Public Health shall transfer to the Medicaid Agency the state funds
1982 attributable to the difference between their costs and Medicaid's routine
1983 reimbursement fee. The Medicaid Agency shall make every effort to maintain
1984 level funding for the adult prosthetic and orthotic program in fiscal year
1985 2027. Any requirements for prior authorization of antipsychotic drugs will be
1986 for the limited purpose of managing off-label utilization. The Medicaid Agency
1987 shall make every effort to provide access for medications prescribed in
1988 accordance with FDA approved indications for mental illness and HIV/AIDS. The
1989 Alabama Medicaid Agency shall not pay for a generic drug that is more
1990 expensive than its brand name drug, net of rebates. The Alabama Medicaid
1991 Agency shall continue to fund and support the PACE program in accordance with
1992 written agreements.

2751 Total Revenue, Department of 463,000 229,166,353 229,629,353
2752 The amounts hereinabove appropriated for the cost of maintenance and operations of
2753 the Department of Revenue are in lieu of any other statutory provisions for the
2754 payment of the cost of operating said Department for collections of the taxes as
2755 authorized by law. Provided, however, in addition to the amount hereinabove
2756 appropriated, there is hereby appropriated to the Department of Revenue all sums
2757 allowed the Department of Revenue by acts of the Legislature as a charge for the
2758 collection of taxes or licenses. The Revenue Department shall not be limited in any
2759 way whatsoever in its ability to utilize or spend its full appropriation and all
2760 sums allowed to the Department of Revenue by acts of the Legislature as a charge for
2761 the collection of taxes or licenses. It is the intent of the Legislature that the
2762 Department of Revenue utilize the appropriations made to it in this act to: (1)
2763 significantly reduce the amount of delinquent taxes owed to the state; (2) employ
2764 sufficient examiners and audit personnel to ensure that taxes owed to the state are
2765 collected accurately and timely; and (3) update its personal computers and related
2766 equipment to become more efficient in the collection of taxes owed to the state.
2767 During Fiscal Year 2027, the Department shall report semi-annually to the Chairs of
2768 the House Ways and Means-General Fund Committee and Senate Finance and
2769 Taxation-General Fund Committee, and the Legislative Fiscal Officer on all actions
2770 taken by the Department in furtherance of these goals. The reports shall include,
2771 but not be limited to: (1) the number and amount of delinquent taxes collected
2772 during the quarter and the number and amounts of delinquent taxes outstanding as of
2773 the end of the quarter; (2) the number of additional examiners and audit personnel
2774 employed during the quarter (not including examiners and audit personnel employed to
2775 replace personnel that retire or otherwise leave state service); and (3) the number
2776 of new personal computers and related equipment put into use during the quarter.

2827 The Alabama SenioRx program shall provide assistance obtaining prescription
2828 medications and shall be expanded to allow comprehensive benefits screening
2829 and application assistance through an Area Agency on Aging designated by the
2830 Department as an Aging and Disability Resource Center (ADRC). It is the intent
2831 of the Legislature that applicants apply through local Area Agencies on Aging
2832 and their provider networks to ensure services are maximized and that
2833 paperwork and inconvenience to the clients are minimized to receive access to
2834 local and public benefits and prescription assistance. The Department of
2835 Senior Services shall report semi-annually to the Chairs of the House Ways and
2836 Means-General Fund Committee and the Senate Finance and Taxation-General Fund
2837 Committee, the Governor, the Director of Finance, and the Legislative Fiscal
2838 Officer. The reports shall include the number of clients served by an ADRC,
2839 the number of unduplicated SenioRx participants, the number of prescriptions
2840 filled, and the estimated value of the drugs provided.

3016 Finance Authority, Alabama Highway Finance Corporation, Alabama Industrial

3019 principal and interest at their respective maturities, of the revenues pledged
3020 for such payment. There is also hereby appropriated an amount not to exceed
3021 $25,000,000 as an annual contribution to the Alabama Transportation
3022 Infrastructure Bank, if needed, for payment of debt service. The Director of
3023 Transportation, with the consent of the Governor and the Director of Finance,
3024 shall have the authority to transfer any appropriation or any portion thereof
3025 between and among subdivisions (a), (b) and (c) of this section whenever such
3026 transfer shall be necessary to assure maximum utilization of federal matching
3027 funds which shall become available. In the event that there shall not be
3028 sufficient funds available for payment of all appropriations hereinabove made,

3030 insufficiency in respect of said revenues accruing to the Department of
3031 Transportation: (1) the appropriation made for Debt Service in subdivisions
3032 (a) and (b) hereof shall be paid in full, and (2) the appropriations from the
3033 revenues accruing to the Department of Transportation that are herein made for
3034 the purposes referred to in subdivisions (a), (b) and (c) except for Debt
3035 Service, hereof shall be allocated among the purposes referred to in said
3036 subdivisions in such order and with such priorities as the Director of the
3037 Department of Transportation shall from time to time direct. The funds

3544 Section 4. In addition to the amounts otherwise
3545 appropriated in this act, there is hereby appropriated from
3546 the several funds in the State Treasury, except the Education
3547 Trust Fund, and in the same proportion as the salaries of the
3548 several State officials and employees are paid, such
3549 additional amounts as may be necessary to pay for a two
3550 percent (2%) salary increase enacted in the 2026 Regular
3551 Session. The additional amounts appropriated in this section
3552 from the State General Fund shall not exceed $16,000,000 for
3553 the fiscal year ending September 30, 2027. The Director of
3554 Finance shall ensure that first priority shall be given to all
3555 State General Fund payrolls, including the payroll of the
3556 Legislature. State agencies shall receive additional
3557 allocations from the appropriation made in this section from
3558 the State General Fund in amounts necessary to increase total
3559 salaries paid from the State General Fund by two percent. The
3560 remainder of this appropriation from the State General Fund
3561 may be allotted by the Director of Finance to those agencies
3562 which receive transfers from the State General Fund.
3563 Section 5. (a) The State General Fund appropriations
3564 in this act anticipate a beginning balance in the State
3565 General Fund for fiscal year 2027, excluding reversions and
3566 adjustments, of $300,120,715. If the State General Fund
3567 beginning balance for Fiscal Year 2027, excluding reversions
3568 and adjustments, is greater than the above stated anticipated
3569 amount, then the first $2,400,000 of the unanticipated and
Page 126

amount, then the first $2,400,000 of the unanticipated and
SB146 Enrolled
3570 unappropriated beginning balance is hereby appropriated from
3571 the State General Fund to state agencies to pay for a one-time
3572 bonus for certain retirees of the Employees' Retirement
3573 System. The Director of Finance shall ensure that first
3574 priority shall be given to all State General Fund payrolls,
3575 including the payroll of the Legislature. State Agencies may
3576 receive additional allocations from the appropriation made in
3577 this section from the State General Fund in amounts necessary
3578 to grant the bonus from the State General Fund. The remainder
3579 of this appropriation from the State General Fund may be
3580 allotted by the Director of Finance to those agencies which
3581 receive transfers from the State General Fund. In addition to
3582 these funds appropriated from the State General Fund, there is
3583 hereby appropriated from the several funds in the State
3584 Treasury, except the Education Trust Fund, and in the same
3585 proportion as the salaries of the several State Officials and
3586 employees are paid, such additional amounts as may be
3587 necessary to pay for the one-time bonus. The funds
3588 appropriated for the bonus in this section are conditioned
